buildbot.slave.commands.TimeoutError: command timed out: 5400 seconds elapsed, attempting to kill
Created attachment 669621
possible fix

There doesn't seem to be anything obviously broken. It's possible that the test runs too slow and it times out. I was able to reproduce timeouts only with very high cpu and IO usage on my system.

This patch extends the timeouts.
